DE CHARLUS — CHARACTER PUZZLES — RED SHOES DUCHESS Albeit simply Sunday autumn, born again, life lay intact me, morning, succession mild days, cold mist cleared nearly midday. change weather sufficient create world oneself anew. Formerly, wind howled chimney, would listen blows struck iron trap keen emotion if, like famous bow-taps C Minor Symphony opens, irresistible appeal mysterious destiny.
